I wear very little makeup but I use it for the bit I do use and all those other things that clutter up my vanity, like my hormone creams (that come in small syringes), perfumes, tiny bottles of essential oils, etc. It is very pretty and I set it out on my bureau, where it really looks as lovely as(and is way more useful than) those expensive mirror trays. I think it's beautiful and useful.<br /><br />It may seem expensive just for plastic, but for not what you're getting because it is so well made. I don't think you can go wrong with this one. The real thing to remember is---SHORT---it's great for short items. Order the company's other larger vanity organizer for bottles of hairspray and other products like that.<br /><br />Highly recommended.<br />*****

  144. Okay, I have to acknowledge that I'm not as thrilled w/ this organizer as I thought I'd be. My disclaimer- I am only advising what works & what doesn't for me, personally. I realize that for some purchasers, this organizer would be absolutely ideal. So I'm not attacking the product. It does fit beautifully in my vanity shelf- the dimensions given are spot on. It is strong & well-made, not too heavy, but is clearly not going to warp or bend like a cheap plastic piece would. Before owning this, I used a Bare Escentuals expandable bag. It was okay- it has nice stretchy rings for holding lipsticks, glosses, mascaras, and two fairly big expandable zippered sections. But it was in a dark color, and sometimes my professional makeup brushes were too long for the case. With using different color schemes all the time, having everything all jumbled together in two big zippered pockets to sort through was a real headache. If I was less of a makeup junkie & only wore one set of the same products day in & day out, it would be easier. But...I am who I am!<br /><br />It depends on the type of makeup brushes, compacts (or containers), size of lip products (especially lipsticks & glosses), and the size of liners used that will determine how happy one would be w/ purchasing this, IMHO. For my purposes, this organizer has some limitations. It holds everything that I have- but not in an ideal fashion. My makeup is mostly Estee Lauder & Lancome, to give you an idea of what sizes of products I'm trying to fit into this piece. I own a moderate amount of brushes, around ten or so. I have full makeup for the eyes (which includes an eyeshadow quad for each tone, a matching darker liner for top lashline & a lighter shade of the same color scheme for lower lashline) in plum/purple, grey/black & brown/beige/taupe. I have lip liner, lipstick & lip gloss in three separate color groups, too- plum/berry, deep peach/coral & cool pink. This is to give you an idea of what I have to store- a packet of pocket tissues (to wipe off brushes after use), cosmetic wedge sponges, one bottle of liquid foundation, one stick concealer w/ a brush to apply it, a pressed powder compact, a large contouring compact (a matte, taupe-y bronzer) & angled brush to apply it, one blush & a blush brush, one Smashbox highlighter compact & a big powder brush to apply that, the aforementioned eye & lip products, two brow brushes, a small pot of eyebrow color, an eyelash curler & two shades of mascara.<br /><br />The lipstick/gloss slots are large, but are VERY shallow. If they come up half an inch, I'd be surprised. This causes my lipsticks to wobble & fall over easily- I really assumed, especially given the cost of this organizer, that the slots would be higher & hold my products more securely. It's hard to see in pictures what I was really getting (even though people have put photos on here full of what they own, which I greatly appreciate & used to decide on buying this). I realize that some people buy products that are oversized. But the lipstick slots could've still been just as big in circumference as they are right now, and yet be high enough to prevent spillovers. I'm not pleased when things are falling over & out of an organizer, obviously. There are enough slots for what I own- but, surprisingly, not much more. My brushes all have to be put together in the left-side largest/highest slot (in the back of the organizer). I'd really prefer an organizer where I could still have that same TYPE of storage, but that separated my face & eye brushes from each other. Unfortunately, there simply isn't room here to do that, so they're jumbled together. There are no long horizontal slots where you can lay a pencil or brush flat, either- my mascara & all my liners (lip & eye) are in the right-side largest/highest slot, by default. I have to lay my eyeshadow compacts, blush & highlighter against each other on their side, vertically held up. There isn't room to store them all flat. I'd honestly prefer to be able to lay them flat, instead of storing them like books on a library shelf, because then I can identify in a flash which product/color scheme it is. My blush & eyeshadow compacts are indistinguishable when on their side, because they're exactly the same compact style. They are identical, except for the description on the back & product within. I'm sure I'll get used to all of this eventually, but again, I'd really prefer to be able to categorize my products by type for ease & speed in my morning makeup routine. Having to search through my entire collection adds time to my routine (which was what caused me to look beyond my BE makeup bag!), and that's exactly what I was trying to minimize. There are also no closed slots within the organizer (possessing a lid, I mean) or drawers. So if you don't use a product often, it'll obviously gather dust, since it's out in the open. However, I knew that when I bought it. I just wish I could've found an organizer of the same size, but w/ a little more thought & care put into the design. I highly doubt that it'd please a professional makeup artist.<br /><br />If I had my act together as a minimalist & only used one color scheme of products, I'd probably like this a lot more. I honestly think it might be better suited for storing toiletries like toothpaste, deodorant & body cream for me personally, not makeup. Time will tell. I hope this review helps!efer to be able to lay them flat, instead of storing them like books on a library shelf, because then I can identify in a flash which product/color scheme it is. My blush & eyeshadow compacts are indistinguishable when on their side, because they're exactly the same compact style. They are identical, except for the description on the back & product within. However, I knew that when I bought it. I just wish I could've found an organizer of the same size, but w/ a little more thought & care put into the design.
